          <a href="/about">
           Silicon Valley Eye Physicians
          </a>
          has grown to two locations in
          <strong>
           Sunnyvale and Santa Clara, CA
          </strong>
          , to better serve the communities with
          <a href="/services/comprehensive-eye-care">

          </a>

          <a href="/eye-conditions">
           eye conditions
          </a>
          including dry eye, cataracts, myopia, and macular degeneration. The
          <a href="/services">
           range of treatments available
          </a>
          at our offices is extensive and can be tailored to suit your needs. Our
          <strong>
           eye doctors
          </strong>
          have developed vision therapy and rehabilitation programs to help improve the eye health of patients of all ages. Our
          <a href="/optical-store">
           optical store
          </a>
          offers a wide range of contact lenses, designer eyeglass frames, and prescription sunglasses to suit your lifestyle while protecting your eyes. For patients who prefer to improve their vision without contacts or lenses, we can also perform
          <a href="/services/lasik-surgery">
           LASIK eye surgery

          <p>
           Dr. Mendelson is a leading optometrist in the field of orthokeratology, which allows patients to correct corneal issues without surgery. He is also one of the few doctors to obtain the title of Fellow of the International Academy of Orthokeratology.
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <!-- Photo Menu Item (3) -->
        <div class="large-4 medium-6 small-12 column photo-menu" data-lucid-group="Photo Menu Item (3)">

     <!-- Content Fragment -->
     <section class="content-fragment" data-lucid-group="Content (2)">
      <div class="row large-collapse">
       <div class="large-6 large-offset-3 column">
        <h2 class="fragment-heading">
         Why Should Patients Schedule a Comprehensive Eye Exam?
        </h2>
        <div>
         <p>
          Early detection of
          <a href="/eye-conditions">
           eye conditions
          </a>
          is the key to ensuring the most effective treatment, and a comprehensive eye exam can help
          <a href="/about/doctors">
           our team of doctors
          </a>
          learn about the health and structure of your eyes. When performing an eye exam, our doctors use state-of-the-art diagnostic equipment to help clearly identify areas of concern. These tools allow us to check for signs of:
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           <a href="/services/glaucoma-treatment">
            Glaucoma
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           <a href="/eye-conditions/cataracts">
            Cataracts
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           <a href="/services/macular-degeneration-treatment">
            Macular Degeneration
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           <a href="/eye-conditions/diabetic-retinopathy">
            Diabetic Retinopathy
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p>
          Identifying these conditions early on can help reduce the risk of permanent vision loss or even blindness. In addition to these advanced tests, our doctors will perform vision testing to identify nearsightedness, farsightedness, or astigmatism and prescribe the appropriate treatment. If you can benefit from contact lenses, eyeglasses, or another treatment, our
          <a href="/optical-store">
           onsite optical stores
          </a>
          offer several options to suit your lifestyle and optical needs.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </section>

     <section class="accurate-fragment" data-lucid-group="AccuRate (1)">
      <div class="row heading-row">
       <div class="large-8 large-offset-2 column">
        <h2 class="fragment-heading">
         Rate Our Practice
        </h2>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="row accurate-description">
       <div class="large-6 large-offset-3 column">
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         We encourage you to join the hundreds of patients who have rated and reviewed their experience at Silicon Valley Eye Physicians.
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="row">
       <div class="large-10 large-offset-1 column text-center">
        <iframe data-full-height="254px" data-small-height="254px" id="accurate-iframe" scrolling="no" src="https://www.docshop.com/accurate/embed.php?style=2&amp;sbid=1593-1005646-fccbfd7504889bd2bf9e9ff98ed06ebe35d17bed&amp;s=http://www.eyelink.com/" style="width: 100%; height: 254px; overflow: hidden;">
        </iframe>
        <script>
         (function(){
   var el = document.getElementById('accurate-iframe');
   if (typeof el == 'undefined') { return; }
   var fullHeight = el.getAttribute('data-full-height');
   var smallHeight = el.getAttribute('data-small-height');
   if (fullHeight == smallHeight) { return; }
   var lastHeight = el.style.height;
   var resizer = function() {
     if (el.clientWidth < 960) {
       var newHeight = smallHeight;
     } else {
       var newHeight = fullHeight;
     }
     if (newHeight != lastHeight) {
       el.style.height = newHeight;
       lastHeight = newHeight;
     }
   };
   setInterval(resizer, 200);
 })();
        </script>
